[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m13[0m[39m:    The protocol tree related functions.<BR>[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m14[0m[39m:    A protocol tree will hold all necessary data to display the whole dissected [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpacket.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m15[0m[39m:    Creating a protocol tree is done in a two stage process:[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m16[0m[39m:    A static part at program startup, and a dynamic part when the dissection [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith the real packet data is done.<BR>[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m17[0m[39m:    The [0m[32m"static"[0m[39m information is provided by creating a hf_register_info hf[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marray, and register it using the[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m18[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mproto_register_field_array[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m function. This is usually done at dissector [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregistering.<BR>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m19[0m[39m:    The [0m[32m"dynamic"[0m[39m information is added to the protocol tree by calling one of [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_...[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m functions,[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m20[0m[39m:    e.g. [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_bytes[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m21[0m[39m:*[0m[35m/[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe evaluation report describes a **global-buffer-overflow** vulnerability in the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWireshark NetBIOS dissector. After analyzing the code snippets, I've identified the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mroot cause:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAt line [0m[1;36m1108[0m[39m in `epan/dissectors/packet-netbios.c`, the code attempts to validate [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe command index:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcommand = [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcommand, [0m[1;35marray_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdissect_netb[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHowever, this validation is incorrect. The `dissect_netb` array has [0m[1;36m33[0m[39m elements [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mindices [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m32[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so `[0m[1;35marray_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdissect_netb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` returns [0m[1;36m33[0m[39m. When the command value [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom the input is >= [0m[1;36m33[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[1;36m0xff[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m255[0m[39m from the fuzzer input[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the MIN macro sets [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcommand to [0m[1;36m33[0m[39m, which is still **out of bounds** for a [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-indexed array. Valid [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindices are [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m, not [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m33[0m[39m.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAt line [0m[1;36m1144[0m[39m, the code directly accesses the array:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msession_id = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdissect_netb[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mcommand[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, pinfo, offset, netb_tree[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWhen [0m[33mcommand[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m33[0m[39m, this attempts to read [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfunction pointer size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m beyond the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marray boundary, triggering the AddressSanitizer error.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Existing Logic to Preserve[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The `dissect_netb` array structure with [0m[1;36m33[0m[39m handlers [0m[1;39m([0m[39mindices [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m32[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m must remain [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Index [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0x20[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m points to `dissect_netb_unknown` which handles undefined [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcommands[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The command extraction at line [0m[1;36m1106[0m[39m and usage at line [0m[1;36m1144[0m[39m must remain the same[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The val_to_str_ext functionality for command name display should continue [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mworking[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. All existing dissector handlers must continue to be called correctly[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Evidence from Codebase[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMultiple examples in the Wireshark codebase show the correct pattern:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `packet-lte-rrc-template.c` lines [0m[1;36m3222[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m3231[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m3238[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m3266[0m[39m: Use `[0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39midx, [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35marray_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvals[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `packet-canopen.c` lines [0m[1;36m774[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m776[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m778[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m786[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m788[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m790[0m[39m: Use `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcs < [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35marray_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39marray[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `packet-ipmi-chassis.c` lines [0m[1;36m564[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m582[0m[39m: Use `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpno < [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35marray_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mboot_options[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAll these examples confirm that the standard practice is to ensure the index is [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstrictly less than the array length, which translates to using `[0m[1;35marray_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39marray[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` when clamping.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mModify line [0m[1;36m1108[0m[39m in `epan/dissectors/packet-netbios.c` to correctly clamp the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcommand value:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Change from:**[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcommand = [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcommand, [0m[1;35marray_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdissect_netb[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Change to:**[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcommand = [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcommand, [0m[1;35marray_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdissect_netb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Implementation Steps[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Locate line [0m[1;36m1108[0m[39m in `epan/dissectors/packet-netbios.c`[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Replace `[0m[1;35marray_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdissect_netb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with `[0m[1;35marray_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdissect_netb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. No other changes are needed[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Justification[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why This is Optimal:**[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Minimal Change**: Only one line needs modification, reducing the risk of [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintroducing new bugs[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Preserves Existing Logic**: All [0m[1;36m33[0m[39m dissector handlers remain functional; the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfix only corrects the bounds check[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Follows Established Patterns**: Matches the pattern used in multiple other [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWireshark dissectors [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlte-rrc, canopen, ipmi-chassis[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Correct Semantics**: Ensures command is clamped to [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe maximum valid index[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor a [0m[1;36m33[0m[39m-element array[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Safe Fallback**: When command >= [0m[1;36m33[0m[39m, it will be set to [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m, which calls [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_netb_unknown` - the intended handler for undefined commands[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How It Addresses the Issue:**[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Prevents the out-of-bounds read by ensuring command never exceeds [0m[1;36m32[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- For the fuzzer input with [0m[33mcommand[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m0xff[0m[39m, [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m255[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m32[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m = [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m, which is within bounds[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Index [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m is `dissect_netb_unknown`, which appropriately handles any command >= [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0x20[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fix maintains backward compatibility with all valid NetBIOS command values [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[1;36m0x00[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m0x1f[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effects:**[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- [0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m expected. The change only affects the clamping logic for invalid command [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalues[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Valid commands [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0x00[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m0x1f[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are unaffected since they're already < [0m[1;36m32[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Commands in range [0m[1;36m0x20[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m0xff[0m[39m will now correctly call `dissect_netb_unknown` at [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindex [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m instead of causing a buffer overflow[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Testing Considerations:**[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer test case [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0x10[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m0x0[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m0xff[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m0xef[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m0xfa[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m0x0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m should pass without [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer errors[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All existing NetBIOS protocol tests should continue to pass[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Edge cases: command values of [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m33[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m255[0m[39m should all be handled correctly[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
